<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">A Collection of Italian Lute Trios
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Single-line Intabulations for 3 lutes unison
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:H%C3%B6ger,_Anton" title="Category:Höger, Anton">Höger, Anton</a>
</td></tr>
<tr class="udelonly" data-display="table-row">

</td></tr>

</td></tr>

</th>
<td>3 lutes
</td></tr></table>
</div>
<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>These "single-line" Intabulations are intended not only for training purposes for students (rhythm, listening sessions, interaction) but can be even small Encores in concerts. -------------- Diese "einstimmigen" Intavolierungen sind nicht nur für Übungszwecke für Schüler gedacht, (Rhythmus, Hörtraining, Zusammenspiel) sondern können auch kleine Zugaben bei Konzerten sein.
</p>
